Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Selected Words
49
Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Foreword
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
Restoration of Subjectivity
<Prayer> Beloved Father, today is October 3, 1971, the first Sabbath of this month. Today is also a day to celebrate the founding of this nation (Gaecheonjeol) and a day to praise the harvest and commemorate our ancestors (Chuseok). While the world celebrates this day externally with these three meanings, we must celebrate internally on behalf of this nation, this world, and Heaven.
Father, please take your seat here. Please look into each of our hearts and command us with your most high and holy authority through our individual hearts, and establish a relationship where we can call you Father, as sons and daughters. This morning, we must not leave any shame before you, our Father, so if we have shortcomings, let us confess them honestly, and in front of countless spirits and ancestors, let us resolve and pledge to become mission bearers who have no shame in fulfilling our historical responsibilities.
Father, we know that each of us has a different past and that each of us bears responsibilities in the present. We are aware that we must continue to go through such responsibilities in our life course, so please look upon us with compassion.
When we compare the values of the past, present, and future, we must realize that the value of the future must be greater than that of the past and present. Therefore, we feel that we must become a sincere offering today, dedicating our intellect and heart to welcome a future that is more valuable than the present. Those of us gathered here must become representatives who kneel before you, standing in for the world, the nation, a religious denomination, and a family, binding together the altar of such sincerity.
When we stand here as representatives, wishing to dedicate ourselves to the world, the nation, and the family, we must do so with the concern that you may see us and say, "Indeed, they are my sons, they are representatives of the family I desired, they are representatives of the nation and world I desired," and that you may appear before us with a joyful heart.
Each of us has a mission appropriate to our position in this era, so especially this morning, may you look upon each individual's heart with fiery eyes, remove all evil conditions, and reject everything that is not good. Awaken in us good hearts and good natures that can align with your ideal, and let us discover that we are not standing alone but standing with you.
As we were born as descendants of fallen humanity, we must overcome this sorrow. We have learned the principle of restoration through indemnity, that we must cross this peak regardless of the sacrifices we must make. We must overcome this peak with all our senses, including our eyes, ears, nose, and mouth, in harmony with Heaven.
We must forget the past we have heard until now, forget the past we have seen, forget all the sensations and natures we have felt, and establish a relationship based on the hope of Heaven, recognizing that we have come this far in our lives. This time must be one where we can evaluate our character and rediscover our feelings about life.
9
It is a lamentable fact that our eyes have not been able to look upon you, Father, and it is a lamentable fact that our ears have not heard your holy voice of love. It is a sorrow that our noses have not smelled the fragrance of your love in the sinless Eden or the scents from the flower garden.
This mouth that has not tasted the fruits of your liberation in your holy garden bears a grievance. When we think of all the feelings we have experienced and all the sensations we have felt in opposition to you, we must realize that we are the descendants of fallen humanity, stained and defiled, and with a sincere heart, we must long to reach that holy and liberated good state, standing there, looking up to Heaven, praising you, and yearning for the day we can hear your counsel and receive your commands.
We must lament that our feelings have not been able to stand in a position where they can be naturalized before you, as we look upon nature as the fragrant garden of blessings you have allowed. We must regret that we have not been able to stand in a position where all our feelings can be naturalized before you.
We must give up the decadent self that has cherished such things until now and learn to long for the original self that Heaven wanted to protect. We are your children who have gathered here to find the way to become such a self. Aware that all our feelings are stained, may our hearts and entire emotions be motivated by you, establishing a connection with you that bears fruit through you.
As we praise everything before you, we must also live a life that can praise the world as a manifestation of your nature, fearing that we may not be able to do so.
Father, as you bestow upon them a new ideology, may they be your children who have emerged with a new worldview, a new national perspective, a new ethnic perspective, a new family perspective, and a new personal perspective. Now, may they firmly establish their distinct identity from the world, affirming that their path is determined, and may they take pride in representing the history that has been filled with resentment due to the fall, and may they take pride in representing this era that is groaning under the suffering caused by the fall, and may they realize that they are those who must praise the form of the nation that will pursue a good world in the future.
10   Restoration of Subjectivity
This exalted self is something bestowed from Heaven, and no matter how evil the flow of thousands of years may be, may they become your children who can protect themselves, fearing that it may tarnish your goodness, and not only protect but also act with the subjectivity of goodness to exercise the authority of judgment over evil. Father, I sincerely hope and desire this.
Father, they do not know what the original heart that their minds envision is like. They do not realize that all the feelings that seep through their senses are not related to you, and that this is a sorrowful fact, an unjust fact, and a tearful fact. If they shed tears through their eyes, let those tears be tears of longing for you, and if there is something that cries out and shouts, let that be the voice of longing for you and wanting to meet you.
If there are feelings experienced in this evil world, if there are any standards that they have felt to the utmost, they must struggle to feel that standard a thousandfold, ten thousandfold, in harmony with Heaven, and we must hate that we have become the descendants of the fall. We must reject all of this. We must also remove such environments.
We must stop the footsteps of our coming Father and, with tears, welcome you, saying, "Father, who has overcome the path of suffering for the sake of finding only my individual self." In a place of despair where we cannot fulfill the ties of atonement and have no hope for tomorrow, there must be a group among the believers on this earth who wish to welcome you with a heart that sympathizes with Heaven and longs for Heaven, believing that only Heaven can be the starting point of all new hopes. If there is even one such person among those gathered here, we know that your coming is not a sorrowful step.
Father, we must feel that our hearts and bodies are born through you. We must realize that all our ways of thinking and ideologies are held through you. If we do not, we will become symbols of Heaven's sorrow and a lamentable fact that can provoke Heaven's loneliness, and we feel this now, so Father, please come to us.
When you, our Father, who knows that we are originally your children, seek us through the heart of your nature, how astonishing it must be! Therefore, even if we have pain in our insufficient selves, we cannot say we are hurting; even if we are wounded, we cannot say we are wounded; and even if there is something ugly to see, we cannot show it to you as ugly. Yet, when we appear with a heart that hopes for your mercy, compassion, and sympathy, you, looking upon our wounds, will see that lonely figure and, with tears of sorrow, resolve to lift us up to a place where you can be comforted, knowing that you wish to bring us to that place. We are hoping for the place where the heart of restoration can be felt, and we are longing for the place where your holiness can be newly connected, so please accept us as your children who can be in that place. Father, I sincerely hope and desire this.
Father, as we reach October 3rd, tomorrow will be October 4th. An unforgettable day in our Unification Church is approaching us. We remember the time 16 years ago when we passed through sorrow and welcomed a day of liberation. We must not forget the past grievances that shared sorrow with Heaven during that time in the history of our Unification Church. We must not forget that we were a group that could rejoice with Heaven on that day. Today, on October 3rd, the day before that, we must remember the merciful Father, the compassionate Father, the forgiving Father. Although we have said for over ten years that we would do so, we cannot express in words how much we have fallen short before you in our lives.
We must not forget that there was a day when we swore before you with fervent hearts. We must not forget the day when we stood proudly before our nation, proclaiming a day of victory and pledging the authority of victory while enduring, enduring, and enduring again.
Father, as we adjust our collars and once again apologize for our past shortcomings, we earnestly hope that you will come to find your children who are hoping for the image of the merciful Father, the compassionate Father, and the sympathetic Father.
O Father, who loves this land of the Republic of Korea, O Father, who comes to this nation, we know that you must not forsake this people, and you know that very well. May we become your children who lament that there is no one to inherit the tears you shed on the path of suffering, and may this gathering of your children who understand that you were a pitiful Father who could not find a place to contain yourself in the midst of persecution be established.
May we become a unification group that knows the situation of the Father, who had to turn away when countless people on Heaven's side fell to the enemy's sword.
Even if we have grievances, we must inherit Heaven's grievances before we express our own. Even if we have sorrow, we must inherit your sorrow before we express our own. If there is a path of suffering, we must indemnify that path by inheriting Heaven's suffering, and we must not become those who think of our own suffering before walking that path. We must not become those who think of our own persecution and loneliness. Father, I earnestly hope and desire that we may be allowed to be your sons and daughters who stand on your side, thinking of how proud you would be of us.
Father, bless this nation and this people on this day. Embrace this land of the three thousand ri, this Korean Peninsula, Father. This nation must be one that manifests your high authority, and may it not become a nation that raises the flag of betrayal and rebellion before you. It must not become such a nation. If there are such evil groups, Father, please remove them.
For the time of Heaven, may there be a group that, while being trampled, struggles to comfort Heaven with tears, so that the lowly may be raised and the lofty may be brought low, following the connections of Heaven, establishing a glorious nation that can proclaim that glory throughout the world, and may that day come quickly through this people.
13
Moreover, on this day, there are young daughters belonging to the Unification Church scattered throughout South Korea. Whenever they see others joyfully celebrating this day and mingling, let them remember their husbands and children. Father, please remember their hearts. If they shed tears, may those tears not be in vain. May your heart be intertwined with theirs, and may your feelings dwell within them.
We are fighting while holding onto this church. Even with our insufficient sincerity, we are striving to set a standard of sincerity, and we are struggling to live lives that fall short of that sincerity. Father, you know that these are the only ones who can represent this nation, so please extend your hand of compassion. If there are daughters shedding tears, let them shed tears with you. Let them not become those who shed tears centered on their own fleshly feelings, but let them remain as a group that sheds tears longing for a new people and a new nation, feeling the resentment of not being able to become a sovereign people who have their own nation, and longing to indemnify the sorrow of the Father who lost Israel two thousand years ago. When that happens, we know that we will never perish, so we ask you to keep us in this way.
I am well aware that you have placed me in this position.  
Father, please maintain this position. For the lonely sons and daughters who are being pushed aside at home, at work, at school, or in society, if there is a place where they are devoted to protecting this denomination and the church, Father, please do not leave that place. I earnestly hope that your heart of mercy will be with them as they struggle to inherit the valley of tears, as they strive to carry on the history of suffering.  
I wish for those who wish to forget everything and possess only you, Father, to not be disregarded by you and to be protected. Every time I stand in such a position, I think of the historical connections you have granted. I know that stepping forward for heaven will not lead to failure. Therefore, I understand that even though they are in a lonely place, they are not pitiful. I earnestly hope and wish that you will personally be with them in that place.  
Father, as they unite and look upon this nation and this world, or as they look upon Christianity, which has inherited the will of heaven, the tears they shed will be holy tears. Even if they shed tears in a place where no one knows, I know that when the time of harvest comes, they will reap. I understand that when spring comes, shoots will sprout, when summer comes, flowers will bloom, and when autumn comes, there will be fruit; this is the principle of heaven. Therefore, regardless of whether anyone sees or not, whether it rains or snows, whether the wind blows or whatever changes in the seasons occur, may our hearts remain unchanged and may we not delay in the struggle to bear the fruit of life. I earnestly hope and wish for this.  
Who are the children gathered here for? Please let there be not a single life that has gathered with thoughts of self or with a heart seeking individual benefit. They are a group that has gathered out of longing for your mercy, love, and compassion that must remain, so the tears they shed must not be in vain. They must shed tears for the sake of saving the nation, the world, and heaven rather than for the sake of individual salvation. May this place become a time that inspires heartfelt sobs while solidifying our hearts, a time that creates connections that can resonate with your heart, and a time that feels like tying new knots.  
Please bless every place where your children across the nation kneel and pray, and protect the lonely groups of unification scattered throughout the world, Father. As they look toward the end of Asia, longing to meet their teacher, and as they shed tears thinking of this Seoul, may your infinite mercy and love be with every place where tears are shed. Even if their bodies are divided, may you embrace them so that their hearts and spirits can live with sympathetic feelings within the realm of unity, and I earnestly ask and wish for you to guide them.  
On this day, let us resolve to make it a day of victory. We must understand how much the countless spirits in the spirit world are longing to hear the cries of liberation from the descendants of humanity on this earth, who are restoring heaven's sovereignty and reclaiming national independence. The closer that time comes, the more we must forget the night even if it is night, and forget the day even if it is day, and only be able to govern day and night with a heart that longs for you, Father. I earnestly ask and wish that only the loyalty to establish your nation remains.  
Please do not let us be a group that comes in vain this morning and returns. I earnestly hope that this time will be one where we are immersed in your mercy, compassion, sympathy, and love, or where we can experience it.  
Please govern all things with your will. Father, please take charge of the remaining days of this year from October. Please tread upon the authority of evil and establish the authority of goodness, so that the time of global glory, where the exercise of judgment can be revealed, may come soon. I pray all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen.  
<Words> We know well that countless humanity living on this earth, including ourselves, is reaching out for something higher than anything else with hope from our current position.  
Humans, regardless of gender or age, pursue something higher and better, whether looking at the historical process, the realities of the times, or the future. We know that anyone, regardless of their social status, has sought and is seeking something higher. We understand that even the most foolish person wishes for the whole to be connected to themselves. We know that our hearts demand a path that connects the individual 'I' to the ultimate standard, the absolute standard.  
No matter what one possesses, when something better exists, they desire it. If something better exists than that, they desire it again. This applies to relative objects or conditions, but it also applies when viewed from the perspective of our individual selves. If we ask how deep the heart we possess is, no one can answer. If this heart is deep, it is unimaginably deep. And when we ask how wide the heart is, if it is wide, we feel that it is infinitely wide.  
When we explore the world of the heart that occupies such an infinite range, there must be a center in that world of the heart. If there is a center in the world of the heart, when asked whether we want to leave that deep center or high center as it is, the answer is no. When there is a higher place centered around the relative world, our individual selves want to relate to it. If there is a supreme being in the world of the heart, the world of nature, we cannot deny that we would also want to relate to that being.  
From the very beginning of the world of the heart to the very end of the relative world through the body, from the starting point of the fundamental to the destination of the ultimate point, we do not want to think of anything without including ourselves. We must understand that it is our human desire to want to establish relationships centered around ourselves.  
The standard of hope presented by the Principle of Unification  
From this perspective, what position are you currently in? Considering what center of our nature exists, how far is the distance to the center of infinite value that has reached me? The path we must take from now on, the path indicated by our principle, includes the restoration of the individual, the family, the tribe, the nation, the world, and the cosmos. It is not enough to just restore the cosmos; we are looking forward to the position where we can establish relative absolute authority centered on love before the absolute being and achieve unity.  
In this regard, we are confident that the standard of hope presented by the Principle of Unification is beyond any standards proposed by all ideologies throughout history. When we think of the whole, before drawing a circle, before drawing a plane, we must draw a line. In drawing a line, or when looking at human nature, there must be a point that serves as the origin of the nature that has started. If that is a point, there must be a destination that humanity desires. If that destination is also a point, there must be a line that can connect it. Should that line be curved or straight? It must not be curved; it must first be straight. We must draw a straight line.  
Can we draw a straight line just like that? If we could draw it just like that, if the origin of all existence came from heaven, then the nouns of heaven's sorrow, lamentation, or pain would not have appeared in history. There would be no need for the framework of religion to arise and worship heaven.  
If there had been a standard that could freely draw a straight line from the origin to the result, then today, God would not be worried. The existing world is supposed to follow that straight line; no existence can have the power to cross that drawn straight line.  
When we see this, if such a standard is established, anyone, any being, is automatically placed in the position of hope and simultaneously in the position of the future hope, but when we see that this is not the case, it indicates that this straight line has not been drawn.  
We can understand that the straight line connecting the standards of cause and effect has not been drawn.  
Then, by whom will this straight line be drawn? To draw a straight line, a center that can always connect the essence of cause and effect is necessary. What is that? As you have learned the principle, we humans are the substantial embodiment that encompasses the spiritual world and the substantial embodiment that encompasses the physical world. The spiritual and physical worlds are summed up around one person. That is why we call humans a microcosm. Saying microcosm does not simply mean a small universe. It means that we occupy the position that can replace the nucleus. Therefore, where must we draw the straight line? The conclusion is that it must be drawn with a person in the center.  
If we draw a straight line on a circle, we draw such a line. Before drawing this central line, there are myriad lines. No one would want to draw such a line. We must draw the highest line. Where is the highest line? There is only one highest line, and that is the line through the center point. The highest line must be drawn here. Only through the center point can the highest line be drawn. (Explaining while drawing on the blackboard)  
The center of the universe is humanity.  
When we look at all existing beings in the world today, they must resemble a circle. The earth is like that, but the universe is also like that. The entire universe is not flat; it follows a circular path. Since the world moves with the relationship of action, it is inevitable that it must have a circular shape.  
God is the same. To be in the position of God, God must also revolve. To revolve, there must be a processual being that can connect the starting point and the destination. That being is one that can represent the whole and determine the position of the whole. What is that being? It is this point. The being that must come to this point is precisely humanity.  
If we cut this in half, one side becomes the spiritual world, and the other side becomes the physical body. If we cut it in half, it becomes up and down, left and right. The front and back, left and right, and up and down do not conflict with each other, nor do they differ in size; they can determine the origin of equality. Where can that be? It is at the center point. Everything is the same. Only through this position can we achieve the unity of the whole.  
Here, the higher is not for the sake of the higher, but for the sake of helping the lower. Likewise, the lower is not for the sake of the lower, but for the sake of the higher. This is how it is. The right side is not for the sake of the right side, but for the sake of helping the left side, and the left side is not for the sake of the left side, but for the sake of the right side. The same applies to the front and back. Rather than serving oneself, we must determine the position of serving the other based on the principle of existence.  
Then, what kind of position is that? It is a position where we can eternally determine what can be judged as right, a position that can establish an absolute standard that no one can deny; that position is the center position, and the boundary line is the central line, which we cannot deny.  
Even when you look at your body and mind, they have separate directions. When we see this, they are different. The body has its own direction, and the mind has its own direction, each having different directions.  
What is the fall? It is widening the gap with the center. What kind of person is an evil person? It is a person whose distance is wide. The wider this gap becomes, the more evil it becomes. The action of expanding the range of deviation from this center point is the action of evil. (Explaining while writing on the board)  
Therefore, there must be an action that seeks to align with the center point, which is the action of goodness. Evil acts to divide infinitely, while goodness acts to unify infinitely. If it is absolute goodness, it must achieve absolute unity, and that unity must go on forever. If there is absolute evil, that evil spreads.  
In that case, individuals will be divided and scattered to the ends of the world. A family that lives without ever seeing the possibility of eternal unity is an evil family. Furthermore, when looking at a nation through the thoughts of national character or patriotism, if the citizens cannot unite, that nation is bound to perish. When we see this, the position where we must establish a comprehensive origin is neither God nor any purpose but our human selves.  
Thus, everything that is originated in heaven must pass through my heart, and all beings that are originated in the external world must pass through my body. This must not be a double position where they cross each other. We must stand on a straight line. Therefore, the path of the way is to reverse the divided humans and bring them closer together.  
Important issues for contemporary humans  
In Buddhism, those who meditate reach a state where they ponder what the heart is, and they reach a level where it seems to exist and not exist at the same time.  
To say that something exists, one must have a relative concept to feel it. One cannot feel it alone. The stronger the relative concept is, the stronger the value of one's existence becomes. The weaker the relative concept becomes, the weaker the value of one's existence becomes.  
Therefore, when does a parent with a beloved child feel fulfillment? It is when the internal connection that can unite the parent and child, that is, the relative relationship, becomes solidified. The more that connection expands, the more fulfillment they feel, rather than anxiety. The more they take on a three-dimensional form, the more fulfillment they feel, rather than anxiety. However, when those conditions become vague, loneliness comes.  
In this light, what is the current age we live in on this earth? It is a time that enters the era of forgetting everything. When we consider where the world is, where the nation is, and where the family is, it also denies those. Furthermore, when we ask where the individual self is, it is a self that exists on an uncertain basis. Because we have not discovered a basis that can be established... It is foolish to establish something from an uncertain position. Therefore, this era of denying even oneself...
is in a situation.
Why is that? It is because it cannot be otherwise. This is because the starting point and the destination are not connected. This is not something that is connected by any origin, nor is it connected by any path that can lead to a purpose; it is just floating aimlessly. Being in such a position, one cannot help but reject everything, asking, "What is a nation, what is the world, what is all this humanitarianism?" If God exists, that God cannot exert any power centered on a person in such a position. Why? Because the more one acts, the more it becomes a minus. It results in a loss. God does not engage in activities that result in loss. The heavenly principles also do not engage in activities that result in loss.

If there is a heavenly fortune that has a certain motivation and goes through a process to find a purpose, that heavenly fortune must go through some medium that can bring the motivation and purpose closer together and shorten the distance. Even though we humans are supposed to fulfill the mission of determining the position of such a medium, if one is in a position where they cannot determine anything, then heavenly fortune will not move through them. For such a person, no matter how much hope one places, there can be no moment of hope.

Even when viewed through the lens of existential philosophy today, it is evident that humans are groaning in the present. The issue revolves around how to pursue human value in this current world. However, no matter how much one tries to find value… one must establish arguments regarding who should be the origin of that value: "Who is the origin of that value? Is it a person, is it a nation?" When delving into such questions, the origin becomes ambiguous. There is no way to determine a definitive standard of value. When considering the conclusion that leads to such thoughts, one cannot help but question where this world is headed in the future. The problem cannot be small.

At this time, when we are crying out against human alienation, we also cannot determine who has alienated humans or whether humans have made themselves that way. We do not even know whether we have been alienated or whether we have made ourselves alienated. There is no solution.

**Return to Subjectivity**
From this perspective, what should humans now recognize? What we need to recognize is that humans cannot stand in the original central position. This must be realized. Humans themselves cannot determine what the original central position is. They cannot be the origin of the starting point nor the result of the purpose. Therefore, the issue of how to recognize the position that connects through the process of internal connection is a much larger issue for humanity.

When looking at the self that is "I," it is undoubtedly a resultant existence, yet we do not know through what it is a result. If we carefully examine the result of "I," we find that the existence of "I" has come through individuals, tribes, nations, and up to the present world. After numerous wars, today’s "I" has been left behind. So, how much suffering and struggle must today’s "I" overcome to raise new hopes and ideals? However, when considering that today’s "I" cannot discover anything to pledge its own resolution to overcome that, it cannot help but enter a state of despair. We must recognize that this is the current anguish of our world.

That is why we must understand what position we are currently in. This position is neither an origin nor a result; it is the position of an intermediary. The intermediary must align with the motivation and align with the result. Without that, one cannot determine their own position. The content of that value cannot be analyzed.

**Restoration of the World of Nature and Individual Value**
Therefore, if God exists, to resolve the path of life today, He must lead us humans to the positions of motivation and purpose. Thus, God has been guiding us through religion until now, emphasizing a life in harmony with the heart. At the same time, He has not told us to live in harmony with this world. He has emphasized the connections of life in the world beyond the end. Even looking at Christianity, there is no teaching that instructs us to live centered on this reality. There is nothing that teaches us to live well in this world. It must always cry out for peace in the heart. "Where is heaven? It is not in this world but in your heart. Heaven exists in the world of the heart, and heaven will be realized at the end." This is the teaching that has been conveyed. The heaven of the end refers to a heaven that is realized in a position that has nothing to do with this world. Therefore, it is not a teaching that instructs humans, who are going through historical processes, about the contents of those historical processes. Religion must originally be like that. If there is a religion that teaches the principles of the process and makes that the standard and purpose, that religion, when viewed from a purely religious standpoint, is a heresy.

We must affirm the world of the heart and pursue the world of nature. What is the value of my individual self in the world of nature? This is the issue. What is the value of my family in the world of nature? We do not know that. We also do not know what our views on the nation and the world are in the world of the heart and the world of nature. Jesus said that heaven is in your heart, yet even Christianity has not been able to determine the specific content of that heaven that is in the heart. Then, how can the heaven of the heart be connected to the heaven of the external world? There are no concrete solutions to this in the scriptures. Therefore, Christianity's inability to find its way at the end is because it stands in such a position. This must be an unavoidable, conclusive position.

Then, what is the heaven of the heart in our world of nature, and what is the essence of heaven? This is the important issue we must raise regarding the future world of nature, the heaven that will come.

**Return to Subjectivity**
So, who is the center that can solve this problem? Of course, it must be through a person, but since a person is neither the origin nor the result of the overall purpose, they must be completely aligned with what can be the origin. In other words, the good must necessarily reach here. If heaven acts, it must come here. (Pointing to a diagram) Where should that action reach? It should not reach the nation first. It must first reach the individual. Before reaching a specific ethnicity, it must reach a specific individual. No matter how global and historical God's providence may be, that providence must necessarily approach through the individual.

What kind of individual is that? It is an individual who serves heaven. In other words, it is an individual who absolutizes God. It is a person who values motivation more than their own life. It is through such an individual that we go. When that individual is confirmed, we go through that individual. It is not that this individual goes like this, but that everything unfolds from here through that individual. (Explaining while writing on a board) Before the center is determined, one must not draw lines in all directions. If one does, it will lead to disaster.

Once, we had a joint worship service between Seobinggo Church and Myeongsudae Church on that sandy beach. At that time, there was a boat collecting gravel, and there was a pile of gravel stacked up. Since I was someone who didn’t eat lunch, I would hide behind the pile of stones during lunchtime. Thinking back to that time...

You know, during youth, such experiences are really necessary. You can think of all sorts of things. As a young man, I had pride and a sense of dignity. Yet, I was isolated from my environment, sitting alone behind a pile of stones while everyone else had lunch, looking at the river and throwing stones... It feels like just yesterday. It feels so vivid. I prayed alone... That was a serious moment. The more serious the environment, the more serious it is. At that time, a woman named Mrs. Son brought me two pieces of bread and a bag of milk, and I still can't forget that. I will never forget that for my entire life. I think I need to repay that.

And then, when I was in prison, I met a young person. It was the first time I met him after entering prison; he opened up everything to me, giving me his food instead of eating himself. I still remember that person. I haven't forgotten his name. I will repay that several hundred times in the future.

Next, one unforgettable incident during the evacuation was when I met a friend from my hometown. At that time, I had just come out of a prison in the North, so my hair was short and I looked terrible. My silk jacket was so black that I had turned it inside out to show the army green lining. When I wore it inside out, it looked like a plain blue jacket. (Laughs) I had worn that silk jacket for two months, so it was in terrible condition. The grease had soaked in, and when it rained, the raindrops would roll off. I arrived in Busan in terrible shape. The roads in Busan are main roads. You can meet people from all over the country. Because it’s a main road, if you go back and forth for a week, you meet everyone. So, feeling lonely in Busan, I wandered around that main road and met a friend from my hometown. That person gave me 10,000 won.

But something unpleasant happened. I thought I would repay that several hundred times; I thought I would repay it several thousand times... Before that, I was someone who didn't even want to meet anyone. 'I will repay you. When the time comes, I will repay you several thousand times.' I was thinking like that, but a few years later, that person's wife came to find me at the Unification Church. At that time, she didn't know I would become the leader of the Unification Church. She thought I was just someone she knew from her neighborhood, but later realized I had become the leader of the Unification Church. She said that we had helped Reverend Moon so much, so now we should be helped in return. I felt very unpleasant. How could a woman come like that... I had hoped to meet her with a heart that would feed and support her children, but she appeared so shamelessly. I can't express how unpleasant that made me feel. I thought it would have been better to die than to face such a situation. It could happen to that person. So, I didn't even meet her. Since I had received 10,000 won at that time, I told her to calculate the interest and quickly pay it back to chase her away. I told her to pay it back yearly as interest. After that, I felt so bad... The standard I had longed for and praised as good, the most stimulating and memorable target during the evacuation period, was completely shattered, and I can't express how bad that made me feel.

I have seen this with the members of the Unification Church as well. I have picked someone and thought, 'This person is coming out like this, let's see where this goes. I will see how far this person goes.' But this person, whom I hoped would become a dragon, turned out to be nothing more than a coward. 'I did that, so why don't you recognize it?' they say. (The recording pauses briefly)

The leader is someone who promises to repay the highest debt to those unforgettable people who have shown compassion for heaven. Do you understand? That’s the kind of person I am. Even though I may cause you hardship on the path of following the will, I am not an irresponsible person. If I cause hardship, I take responsibility for it. If I can't take responsibility on earth, I will take responsibility in the spirit world.

Therefore, I believe that those who make such pledges with me are blessed people. I am someone who will never betray. Once I believe, it’s absolute. I cannot live while being indebted even a little. That’s my nature. God is like that. What kind of being is God? He cannot stand being indebted. If He gives ten, He wants to repay several hundred or several thousand times. Do you understand? Your restoration must be like that.

Among the comrades here or among those you meet while evangelizing in the regions, it must be like that. Evangelizing is absolutely not a bad thing. It expands the foundation of hope to pray for those you have met in difficult times throughout your life. So whether you go to prison or face suffering... Those who can form such connections are rare in normal times.

When you see this, the position of serving others based on the public standard centered on God is extremely precious. When you think of this, if you stand in a place where you can love God and love the world, you will never fail. In such a place of cause and effect, standing at such a standard, if you can discern things on either side and stand in the center, representing humanity and standing in the position of God, centered on the vertical heaven and the horizontal world, if you go out with the heart to build a bridge to move this world into a new world, how fulfilling would that be? It starts from here, spreading from such individuals. (Writing on the board)

Blessed husbands and wives must love each other in a position that represents the world and the heavenly earth. If this standard can be established today in our lifetime, where can we find greater happiness?

<Words> You have attended here as members of the Unification Church. Furthermore, you are responsible leaders in the Unification Church's business fields, working in your missions since October 9, 1971 (Saturday), at the Central Training Center (Sutaek-ri).  
* These words were spoken at a national business directors' training session and were also published in the January 1976 issue of <Unified World> (published on January 20, 1976). The beginning part of the prayer was not recorded.  
In this context, your position is not an ordinary one within the Unification Church. You are undoubtedly in a leadership position.  
The position of business directors  
The position you stand in has both an upper and a lower aspect. There is also a sequence of precedence and a left and right. Above you are connected to the Teacher's family, and your family is linked to the families of the three great representatives on the left and right. Regardless of height or depth, you are in a shared realm of destiny, each with your respective responsibilities, pledging to offer good returns before Heaven. This is the position you currently occupy.  
When you think this way, is the position you occupy solely for the Unification Church, or does it only apply to the Unification Church? No, it does not. Considering the society and environment we live in today, such a position has not yet been established. It is not a position that can serve the Unification Church, nor is it one that can serve you.  
When the Unification Church tries to serve itself, phenomena of division, conflict, and persecution inevitably arise. Moreover, although you have become members of the Unification Church, when you look at your family, there are wives and parents there. When you pledge your mission as individuals, is there an environment where your wives can support you? It cannot be said that everyone is in such a position. And when it comes to your children, can they stand in a position to support you? That cannot be said either. Are your parents, spouses, or siblings, who are connected by blood ties, in a position to support the path you are taking? That is also not the case.  
When you think seriously about this, it is a fact that even though you are currently a member of the Unification Church, the position you occupy is not one that is guaranteed, defended, or praised by the environment. Given that the environment seeks to condemn you and your family does not welcome you, you cannot help but feel lonely.  
Oh, my homeland, shine forth!  
However, it is not possible to sever ties with the environment, nor to cut off your family, society, or country. If you were to leave your family, your country, and the world to go out with your own claims to joy, if that does not represent your family, you would become someone who receives historical condemnation regarding the past, present, and future. The longer you walk that solitary path, the more you will encounter results that can only be condemned, rather than something meaningful in the historical process. Therefore, if you go with a mindset that dislikes the past, dislikes the present, and dislikes the future, that path will naturally come to a halt.  
However, if you later realize that the path you took has trampled over your family, and that you represented that environment, or that you represented that country, if you walked a lonely path to go that way, the longer and more difficult that path is, the more your entire family will abandon their dignity and surrender with tears before you, and the environment will also surrender in such a position, and the country will also be able to surrender in such a position. We cannot overlook that there are these two paths. You are walking with a sense of mission between these two paths.  
The issue of the starting motivation  
Then, what is my starting motivation? Where should I begin? Is it for myself or for others? If you stand on the basis of starting for your own happiness, the environment that appears will be a source of suffering. If your steps are centered around yourself, when your family opposes you, that family becomes an environment of suffering, and when the country opposes you, the country becomes an environment of suffering.  
However, if you stand in a position to sacrifice your own self for the sake of the whole, then you are not harmed by the opposing environment. Rather, if your family opposes you while you are going out for the sake of the whole, the value of that path you take to sacrifice for the whole will change in content because of that opposition from your family. Even when going for the sake of the environment, if that environment opposes you, the value of the path you are taking will shine even more brightly because of that opposing environment. Furthermore, even when going for the sake of the country, if that country opposes you, although it may currently be in conflict with you, when the time comes in the future when it can be better, it will surely welcome you. When you step out to sacrifice for the country, the greater the opposition from that country, the more it will be determined as an absolute standard that can surrender before you.  
Therefore, the question of whether it is public or private arises. What is public? It is to think of others and to think of something greater. Then what is private? It is to think of oneself and to think of something smaller. There are these two paths in walking the path of the will. Among those who stand on the path of the will, there are two types of people. There are those who walk the path of the will but do so for their own benefit, and there are those who walk the path for the benefit of the whole. You are likely walking one of these two paths.  
How much have you loved the will?  
In this regard, the question arises of how much you have loved the will. If you have loved the will enough to abandon your beloved wife or to love others enough to abandon your children, then that person can qualify to receive a better wife and better children. Conversely, if you cannot love the will more than your own children or wife, that person will end up with worse children, not better ones, and worse wives, not better ones. Additionally, if you have loved the will more than any organization you love, that person can receive a better organization than the one they loved, but if they could not love the will more than that organization, they cannot receive an organization greater than that. From there, the path is blocked. No matter how hard that person tries, the path that connects to the country will be blocked.  
When you think about this, if you resolve to walk the path for the sake of the country, even if it means sacrificing the country, you will qualify to receive a country greater than that one, but if you do not do so, you will not be able to receive a country greater than that. This is an undeniable principle.  
When you decide to walk the path of the will for your own sake, you will not discover values greater than yourself. However, when you pursue a better version of yourself by sacrificing your current position, you will discover a path that is better than your current self. You must be certain that you are standing before these two paths.  
When viewed in the context of the Unification Church, there is a path that can be better, as well as a path that can be worse. If you can only walk a path that descends below your current position, you are on a path that leads to a worse place. When you rise above your current position and sacrifice for something greater, you can find a better path. Thus, the past is not the issue; the present is the issue.  
When viewed in this light, whose will is it? It is not a will just for us. It is not a will just for the Unification Church and Teacher Moon. If that will were only for Teacher Moon of the Unification Church, it would end with meeting Teacher Moon. It is a will that transcends Teacher Moon of the Unification Church. If there is an Absolute Being, that will must be the will of the Absolute Being.  
Moreover, when we look at the ideal world from the perspective of that Absolute Being, that ideal world cannot be centered solely on the limitations of earthly existence. When we look at a will that can transcend limits, even if we lose the world, we can become a person who possesses something greater in the inner aspect.  
Such a person, no matter how cruel, no matter how severe, no matter how high the persecution, can remain someone who can overcome that persecution. In other words, when you carry a greater ideology and a greater will, the standard of weaker wills will be encompassed within that. Therefore, a person must have a lofty ideal. In that regard, is there a greater ideology than the unification ideology that has appeared throughout world history? In that sense, the unification ideology can be said to be the highest ideology.  
If you want to find the significance of attending the training session  
Today, we see that the ideologies of democracy and communism are clashing on a global scale. In such a situation, we are in a position where we cannot hope for anything and cannot trust anything. However, standing in a position where we possess the content to criticize and respond to this is the point of higher hope that is the unification ideology.  
Therefore, we must transcend the democratic world and the communist world with this ideology. To transcend the democratic world and the communist world, there are paths that the democratic world cannot take, and the Unification Church must be able to take those paths, and if there are paths that the communist world cannot take, the Unification Church must also be able to take those paths. Then, is there a vanguard among you who can pass through individuals, families, tribes, nations, and reach the world? This raises a question.  
Where do we want to go? It is not this place where we are receiving training. Where do all of humanity want to go? It is to a place greater than this one. It is to a higher place. Why have you come to this place? You did not come to become lower than the hopes you had at that time, but to become higher. Education is not received to become worse. It is received to become better. Therefore, you have come here to become higher. Judging by your true intentions, it is a fact that you have come here to elevate yourselves. If you have come here to be educated to become higher, you should be able to say, "I have become higher than before." That is how it should be. If not, there is no significance in your coming here.  
It may be uncomfortable to follow what the headquarters has instructed. This is a place where you may have more of a rebellious spirit than a spirit of compliance. If a rebellious spirit arises and you follow it, a war of attrition will ensue. When the spirit of compliance becomes strong, progress occurs, but when the conditions for struggle arise, a war of attrition begins.

In Rome, there is a catacomb that is 20 kilometers long. This cave was where Christians lived for four hundred years during the era of tyranny, preserving their faith. There are no benches there. The walls of that cave become graves. When a mother or father dies, they simply place the body there, and even if it becomes a skeleton, they live their lives eating and surviving in that cave. Even now, if you go there, there are shelves lined up. Is there anywhere else to make a communal grave? Outside the cave…

Looking at that, we see that our Christian ancestors were great. It was truly a skull cave. Even in such a pit of death, they planted the truth, rooted themselves in such a miserable place, felt the pulse of life, and praised God. How astonishing must God have felt at that time? That is why the Roman Empire had to fall. It had to become food for Christianity. The longer it lasted, the more the spiritual world was mobilized, and centered around the global situation, it began to develop all at once. Do you understand?

The Unification Church is the same. In the future, just try capturing and killing Unification Church members in the North. The more you kill one, two, three people… the more the ideology of the Unification Church will take root everywhere. When thinking about this, who should go to die first in the North? The leader should go first, right? "No." Then who should die first? "We will die." If there is no one among you who will die, then the leader must die. The leader does not feel sorrow in dying.

If you do not enter into peril, not only will you not be saved, but the Republic of Korea will also perish. What will happen when the people of the Republic of Korea are all destroyed? You must hope to enter there. If you sacrifice there, a new historical explosive force that can unite the nation will emerge from there. You must become the footsteps of a generation that can say, "Let’s go! Let’s kill!" Without that path, there is no way to achieve it, so if there is a son of heaven who says he will achieve his purpose through that path, he must be a son who can melt God's heart, bones, and flesh all at once. The traditional thought of national liberation will sprout from there.

Moreover, the idea of patriotism and the idea of loving the nation must be left as a higher and more valuable traditional thought that should be inherited from our ancestors during the time of national liberation. We must think about that.

The vanguard of national liberation
To lay the path for the eternal heavenly ideal that can shine for a thousand years, it cannot be done with a smooth game. "Even if our bones are ground and our flesh is torn, let us overcome the path of suffering. Even if it is harder than breaking through a cave, let us overcome the path of suffering." Only with such a resolution can you be called a man who has established dignity in this era. If you are born without inheriting such a heart and without having the conviction of that heart, and cannot pledge victory for tomorrow, then it would be better for such a man to die. What good is it to love your wife and children like that?

What kind of person can be the vanguard of the new morning of national liberation? What kind of vanguard does the nation want to welcome? When asked, "What kind of sons and daughters do you want to welcome in the bright coming nation, and how do you want to welcome loyal patriots and virtuous women?" the nation wants to welcome those who are burning with such resolution, who would dedicate their lives even if it means burning them away, and who uphold the value of traditional loyalty as an infinite value, and who pledge to walk the path of death. Isn't that the attitude of the nation that is coming? When I appear before that nation, what kind of attitude should I have? I must resolve that I should not be an utterly shameful self. I must not do that.

Looking back at the 20-year history of our Unification Church, there is much sorrow. The leader has much sorrow. To establish a single tradition, to not stand in a conflicting position before the righteous path that the nation is seeking, regardless of who opposes it, I will go, even if the times change, I will go. **3) Our Nation and Our Mission**
**<Prayer>** Father, when we think about how much effort You put into bringing forth one son and how many costs You bore, the more we realize that it is not something we can think of within our personal scope, the more we must recognize that we are in an era where we must fulfill a serious providential mission. 

Father, please remember the children gathered here. We, who are gathered under the care of a Father who longs for the image of one son, must not become a source of concern for You. We must become the very son You are seeking, and we must become the embodiment of the beauty transformed into the heart of the nature You desire, and we must be the subject of love. 

The more we realize that Your standard is not to find people like us, the more we must recognize our shortcomings and stand in a position to urge the mission of the future, lamenting our inability to uphold Your dignity and face. 

When we reflect on how much we long for You, how much we admire You, and how earnest we are regarding the path of Your will, the more we realize that we should be standing in a place significantly different from where we are today. The stronger our desire to present our inadequate selves before You, the more we must have a heart that seeks Your compassion, mercy, and forgiveness. 

Father, You have come to find good families by gathering individuals like these, and You have come to find good tribes. This makes us realize the astonishing fact that You have indeed had to toil for 6,000 years.

Therefore, may Your heart of compassion resonate within our hearts and allow us to regain our position in the nature of our being. 

The heart that longs for the homeland, the heart that seeks the heart of nature, and the heart that yearns for the original embrace of the Father must be stronger than anything else. We must feel once again that this will be the standard by which we can discern the crossroads of life and death. 

Father, among us, there are family members who have been following this unique path for over ten years, but it is not the length of time that matters; rather, it is how our relationship with You has developed and how that connection has been established that is important.

Father, while blaming our unworthy and insufficient selves, we have gathered here longing to be holy victorious sons and daughters, so please remember the children who have attended this gathering.

When we understand this, we feel the need for a heartfelt desire to repay that grace and to become one with You, so please do not leave us as we are. 

We have entered the Unification Church and have our own understanding of what the Unification Church is and have our own faith about who God is, but we must understand that You are not someone who exists within the limits we know. 

The more we understand this, the more we realize that You are the one who is pitiful, and that You are in a place so pitiful that we cannot even say that we are pitiful. You are the one who has taken responsibility on the front lines of fierce struggles, and we must feel once again that this is not the degree of misery we know, nor the degree of overcoming, nor the degree of struggle. 

We are living centered around human-to-human relationships, yet we often fail to perceive whether the spiritual world exists or not. Even though You are present, we often fail to find the emotional connection to whisper deeply with You. 

When we think of how we have not transcended our own self-awareness while having the admiration to hold You in our hearts, we realize that we should not be the kind of children who come to find You. We have not realized how much You long for us and how earnest Your heart is in seeking us, so please allow us to understand. 

On the other hand, while we have spoken of the existence of Satan, we have not experienced it. When we desire good things and wish to speak and act with goodness, there is an enemy who seeks to block that path, and there is an enemy who lies in ambush to hinder our way and lead us astray.

We must do so for ourselves, for our families, for our tribes, for our nations, and for the world. We must reaffirm that we stand on the path of suffering to break through the evil forces that remain within the earthly realm under the powers of the air. 

If we do not have You, we are a pitiful group. If we do not have You, we are a group that cannot find a place to belong. If we do not have You, even the desire to live becomes an empty feeling, and we must understand this. 

When we ask who will take responsibility for the global authority of the enemy surrounding our ignorance, we must acknowledge that we, the fallen, cannot take responsibility. 

Then, when we ask who will save us from this environment, we realize that it is not our parents who gave us birth, nor our siblings, nor our teachers, nor the sovereign of our nation. 

When we think that there is no one under our command who can look toward the world on the ground and the flat surface, we must only look up to heaven and, in place of Your heart of admiration, with a serious heart, feel the loneliness of deep emotion and sigh, crying out, "Father! Please come quickly. Have compassion on this appearance." 

We realize that there is no other way to break through the enemy's authority than to feel this way through our lives. 

In our lives, we thought that yesterday's friends were today's friends, and that yesterday's parents were today's parents, and that the couples and children we lived with yesterday were our true couples and children, but that was not the case. 

Yesterday's parents have become today's enemies, yesterday's spouses have become today's enemies, and yesterday's beloved nation has become today's enemy. We often fail to realize that we cannot break through this path without recognizing this.

When we think that we must pledge to walk this path and practice it to suppress the realm of death and pave the way for victory, we understand that an individual cannot do so without sacrificing their family, and a family cannot do so without sacrificing their tribe.

<Word> When a person does not have the foundation that Heaven desires, they appear small. They become pitiful. At this time, the standard for being pitiful may vary in countless ways. When looking at any individual, they may have a father, a mother, an older brother, and a younger sibling. There may also be those who have no siblings or parents but possess worldly possessions. There may be those who are rich in material wealth, while others may not have such wealth. In this way, the standards differ in various forms.

When we think about relative conditions, there must be both a subject and an object. And they must give and take. Giving and taking is not just a simple exchange. Right? That’s why a true filial child appears only after death. Is that correct or not?

Among the dead, there may be those who died while going to show filial piety. There may be filial children who died while seeking medicine for their sick parents. Some may go seeking medicine with their own money, while others may go seeking it after borrowing money. The more difficult it is, the greater the value becomes. Isn’t that right?

So, if there is someone who died while going to seek medicine with their own money and someone who died after working hard for three months to borrow money to seek medicine, who would rise to the position of being a model of filial piety? “The latter.” Yes, that’s obvious. Because of that, restoration is possible. The more complicated, difficult, and miserable the content is, the more it can appear as something good.

What is better, dying while going to seek medicine or dying after preparing and administering the medicine? Dying while administering the medicine is better, isn’t it? When you look at it this way, the more difficult the content, the higher the rank in the category of filial piety. There’s no objection to that, right?

Among those who died while showing filial piety, let’s say there’s someone who died with a hole in their head from a bullet and someone who died after being blown to pieces by a bomb, leaving no bones or skin intact. In other words, if someone died without leaving a grave and someone died leaving a grave, if they died in the same position and the same circumstances, who would be the model of filial piety? Who would you choose as a model? Would you choose the one who left a grave? If they died in the same position and the same circumstances, who would be the model? Would you choose the one who left a grave? The one who left a grave, or the one who didn’t? “The one who didn’t leave a grave.” What do you mean they didn’t leave a grave? They didn’t leave one. It’s obvious they didn’t leave one.

That’s why only those who want to die can remain. Let’s say there is a filial child who was born into extreme poverty and lived their whole life without ever wearing a proper outfit, only wearing pants through spring, summer, autumn, and winter. When Jesus asked Peter, do you think he asked gently, “Simon, son of John, do you love me more than these?” Or do you think he had a grim expression and said, “You rotten traitor, you!” He asked three times with a face that no one in the world has. Mr. Moon of the Unification Church also has many enemies among the established church pastors. Forgiving them is not because I am essentially a good person. Jesus said, “If someone strikes you on the left cheek, turn to them the other cheek.” Do you think he said that because he liked it? God's Ideal
Time has passed a lot, but if I keep talking like this…. I would like to finish within 30 minutes, but if I do that, it will be boring for the Unification Church. Has it been about an hour and a half? It has been an hour and a half.

Look. In the world, even to find material things, people have put their necks on the line and wars have broken out, right? Isn't that so? Wars have broken out over material things, causing people to live and die, and nations to fall, right? Isn't that so? To find a loved one, such things must also happen. Isn't that right? There are many wars fought for the sake of loved ones. Isn't that so? Then, for the sake of finding God, there must be a struggle of dying and perishing. If that does not happen, it has no value. Therefore, historically, until now, the struggle of life and death has been intertwined around Christianity. Isn't that so? Christianity must unite and stake their lives on it.

Now, what happens at the end? After finding God, we must find people. Isn't that so? We must find people in unity with God and ourselves. Until now, God has not been able to find people. After finding the man that God likes, we must work together with God to find the woman that God likes. After finding the woman that God likes, who must she find in unity with God? She must find a person, right? So, does a woman find a woman? No, she must find a man. That's how it is. It is inevitable.

After finding the man and woman that God likes, what must we find next? We must find valuable things. Isn't that so? We must find material things. That is the object of human desire. Looking at this, it does not divide everything; after finding God, we must find the family that God likes, and based on that family, we must find all things that God likes and live a life centered around them. Do you want this, or not? This is God's ideal.

In other words, there is a time of bearing fruit. After bearing fruit, there is a time of harvest, and after harvesting, there is a time of storing seeds, that is, the time of the seed. We can see that flowers also go through such a process. There is a time of birth, a time of growth, a time of maturity, and then a time of harvesting; this process is inevitable. At the end of this process, there is a period of trial in which new life can emerge.

If we think of this in terms of the seasons, we can see spring as the time of resurrection. Summer can be seen as the time of growth and development. Autumn is the time of harvest, and winter is the time of trial. The same can be said for a day. Morning is the time of departure, the day is the time of activity, and then evening is the time when everything can be determined in results. Evening corresponds to the autumn season, and night corresponds to the winter season. We understand that this is how things are.
