Those who entered the Unification Church in the 1960s said, "Back then, the teacher raised us all. Those were good times. Now what..." (laughter) It's like a strange world. Back then was spring. In baby terms, it was the time of breastfeeding and changing diapers. As we grow and go to elementary school, we need to be trained socially, so we have to make social contacts, and then we say, "Oh, I don't want to!" Just because you're going to university doesn't mean you're going to have fun, right? Is there anyone who enjoys studying? You study because you have to. Isn't that right? Raise your hand if you enjoy studying. Do you enjoy taking exams? You do it because you have to. 

So, I have no choice but to make you take exams. The issue is not just handing out the test papers. It's about delivering a notice saying, "Now, go around the Korean Peninsula. Dig tunnels." To build a nation, to build a kingdom in the future, there must be something like driving stakes and erecting a framework, right? 

To build a bridge, even in winter, you have to tear down mountains and stack stones on top of the ice. Why do you stack stones? It may seem crazy to stack stones on ice in winter, but when spring comes and the ice melts, it will all sink and become a mountain in the water. When you think about that, the person who stacks stones on the ice is a wise person. Isn't that right? Yes, isn't it? That's how it is. But you all think, "Oh, there's no water, the ice is frozen, why are they stacking stones? I really don't get it!" That's the situation. 

Where will you finish your end? Look, do you think the Unification Church would still exist without the teacher? If the teacher leads from the front, you might say, "Oh, here we go again. The teacher is lucky to have such a fate, but we don't have that fate, so we can't do it." Is there anyone who wants to have a bad fate? Who wants to live a hard life? Just being alive is hard. Even though you are sitting here now, being alive means you are sitting here, suppressing the power of death in the battle between life and death. On a day when you breathe wrong, the power of death says, "You've fallen into my grasp." 

So, there is infinite power that suppresses me, and the natural forces of the universe are acting to cultivate the power of my life. Do you feel that the pressure of one atmosphere of air is keeping your body, your shape, intact? Have you ever thought, even in your dreams, "The force of one atmosphere is pushing like this"? When that disappears, everything will fly away, right? Isn't that right? Yes, it is. But in reality, no one feels it. It's the same. Have you ever felt that beneath your life, there is a foundation of power that suppresses death protecting you? When that collapses, it will all come crashing down at once. 

With such a life, where will you fall? Would you prefer to die in the enemy's upper room? Would you prefer to die in the enemy's upper room, or would you rather die in the enemy's bathroom? Dying in the bathroom is better than dying in the upper room, and dying in the bathroom is better than dying in the yard, and dying in the yard is better than dying in the front yard, and dying in the front yard is better than dying in the enemy's field, and dying in the field is better than dying in the rice paddy. Do you understand? The closer you get to the enemy when you die, the worse it is. Isn't that right? Yes, isn't it? 

So, the world you are living in now is the enemy of God, isn't it? "It is the enemy." Do you really know that? "Yes." Do you know that? Do you know it's the enemy? This world of death, this land is the enemy of God. 

Then, do you live in the enemy's upper room or the lower room? Which room do you live in? Since the owner is the enemy, you can't live in the main room, so you live in the upper room or the love room. So, where do you plan to die? "Where will I die? I'll die where I was born." So, in the end, you will die either in the enemy's upper room, the love room, or the back room. You will die in the enemy's neighborhood. You will die in the enemy's country. Is that good? You will die in the enemy's world. Think about that. It makes you shiver. 

So how will you escape this? "Before I die, I must cross the enemy's border and go to the place where the mountains and rivers of my country, which have been waiting for me, are located. If I can't cross that border and die while crossing it, I must at least let my head cross the border even if my body can't." 

So when you say you've crossed the border, you should think, "This land is better than that land's throne. This land's shack is better than that land's palace. Even if this land treats me like a beggar and like an enemy, it's better than that fallen individual who raised me in the enemy's land." Have you thought about that? If Unification Church members had such ideals and thoughts, would they feel that "even if the people here make my life difficult, it's better than the parents who raised me in the enemy world"? Would they feel that "even if I can't eat or live well here, it's better than living well over there"? Would they think, "Even if I rot in this land, or if the neighborhood dogs eat me and the insects gnaw at me, it's better than the luxurious grave over there"? This is a serious issue. 

Today, Unification Church members must not die within this boundary. Even if I have to suffer with a naked body, with my legs scratched and cut, even if my head and body are covered in blood, the serious issue, the ultimate issue is how to get my body over the 38th parallel and die. 

If there is a heavenly protection that allows me to live with a tradition of yesterday and today on the path of restoration that I hope for, isn't that a glorious place to boast about in history? When the power of death surrounds me, if there is even one person who can sympathize with me when I shed tears, isn't that glory? When I think of that, isn't it a grievance that South Korea is not like that, and isn't it a grievance that the neighborhood we live in is not like that? Yes, within this circle of grievance, I accept that I will die. 

The Unification Church bears the mission of a new history. So, what position are you in? As the time draws near, the 38th parallel is approaching. When the ideal you aim for comes closer, there is danger here. The danger of the nation intersects, the danger of the church intersects, the danger of the family intersects... When everything is aligned in a straight line, representing the entire people, how will you respond? You must become someone who can mercilessly break through that. If not, I must cross the border. 

If I can eliminate that fight and cross the border, there may be glory waiting for me to receive the title of a loyal subject, but before that... If I die before that country comes, I will leave behind the conditions of grievance, so I must cross the 38th parallel of death no matter what.
In today's world, where victory cannot be determined through fighting, I must be the one to cross the 38th parallel. This is the path of the return. Therefore, there are no days that are not serious. Even when we laugh, we cannot laugh freely; through our laughter, we become the focus of the enemy's attention. Even when we live, we cannot live freely, and the stage where we can be invaded by the enemy is publicly open all around us. 

That is why we must control ourselves and prepare ourselves, and on this boundary line, preventing the sorrow of the defeated is the destiny that the Unification Church, which bears the mission of a new history, must follow. Therefore, when we see this country being corrupted, this country being chaotic, and this country being confused, we should not be disheartened by it; rather, we should think that the more it is so, the more our time will come. 

Today, the villains who dream of world domination centered around the world's focal point are already facing a situation where their strength is broken, and they must bow their heads due to the cold winds. At this time, we must pledge that we will mobilize our forces and become the final offensive to crush the enemy's stronghold. However, those who approach each day with a habitual mindset will fail. Those who spend their daily lives in the same way will become the defeated and the left behind. 

When we think about this, we must ask ourselves, "What era am I facing in the Unification Church? Is it the spring era, summer era, autumn era, or winter era? Am I a new seed that has condensed the four seasons into my own life force? Even if I have to sacrifice, my family will remain as a group that can connect to the glorious heaven that can greet the spring day for thousands of years. I will emerge as such a figure. I fight to leave a decisive factor in this era. I exist for that purpose." 

We must be able to say this. The time has come for us to do so, and the question is how we will absorb and overcome the environmental conditions that are approaching us. This is not an ordinary issue; it is a solemn one that you must understand and commit to. 

When the day flows away, it means death at that place. On the day of collapse, on the day of dying, we will have no choice but to become the food of the dogs that guard the master and the garden in the enemy's country. We must not become the death that nourishes the dogs that enter and exit the enemy's door. This is a serious issue. It is not just words; it is a fact. God has been pledging such a solemn and decisive connection through our life journey. 

You will be so, and your descendants will be so, and when we think about the destiny of our Unification Church today, if there is a way to integrate and resolve that destiny in our time, how will we condense it and bring it to fruition? When we look at the current normal times where North and South are intersecting, what should we do? Without resolving to march forward toward the ultimate purpose with the highest resolution and the greatest determination, you will become the left behind. 

No matter how lush the leaves hanging on the tree are, no matter how abundant the flowers that have bloomed are, once they fall, they can only become fertilizer. They become fertilizer at the place where they fall. For the Unification Church to become a greater Unification Church in the future, it must recognize that becoming fertilizer is the norm if it has become leaves or flowers. Ultimately, what this means is that when I go, I must be someone who even gives fertilizer to the Unification Church. Otherwise, I cannot fulfill the mission of being a normal leaf. If I become a leaf that flies away when the wind blows, I cannot fulfill the mission of being fertilizer as a leaf. 

Therefore, when I die, I must become a being that can be remembered in the history of the Unification Church. After I die, I must remain as an object of mourning and admiration. 

When we consider these issues, we must break through and escape the foundation of resentment born in the realm of death. When we look at the historical process through which humanity has been groping in the dark from countless ancestors to the present, those who slow down their steps at this moment, where we have presented a common goal and direction, will inevitably not be able to avoid the fate of being left behind and the sorrow of the defeated. 

When we think about how our ancestors fell and disappeared so miserably, we must realize that it is a historical inevitability that we cannot help but stand there and become participants, even if we die. This is a serious issue. 

You must think about the place where you love your wife or husband, the place where you embrace and love your children, the floor you lie on, the country you live in, and the world you live in. Therefore, when we think about the Unification warrior who seeks to present a new direction and new purpose through the organization of tribes, nations, and the world, will we greet this with sadness or joy? If we greet it with sadness, we will not see the fruits. We absolutely will not see the fruits. 

In any difficult environment, we must have the autonomy to absorb it with joy and hope and bear fruit even in those difficult places. 

No matter how difficult it is, be the one who blooms the flowers of a new history. 

The other day, while going from Cheongpyeong to Hongcheon, I saw a rocky island. At the top of that rocky island, there was no soil, yet a pine tree was growing in the crevices of the rock. It was small in height but had lush branches. Seeing that, I thought, "You are admirable." Even though it must be dry at the top of the rock, its branches were green. Upon closer inspection, I found that a river was flowing below. "Ah, there was a way to continuously absorb moisture through the crevices of the rock." I realized that the Unification Church must be like that. 

In a way that is inexplicable, with a supply line of life that others cannot understand, it may be extremely narrow and thin, but just as it can be so green through that supply, the Unification Church will also become green in that way. That is why the Unification Church has laid a global foundation while being persecuted. "Even if ten years, a hundred years, or a thousand years pass, we must have a source of perpetual supply that does not dry up..." This is what we have thought and come this far. 

Do not complain about the difficult position. Even in that difficult environment, if there is a gap where roots can spread, if there is an underground stream flowing beneath, do not worry. When it grows brightly there, there will be a way to be moved to the courtyard of the master’s house, to emerge as the most precious tree among trees. Isn’t that so? 

Today is UN Day. If we look at October 24 with our numbers, 3 times 8 equals 24. The number 10 is the number of heaven, so centered around heaven, when we say 3 times 8 equals 24, the number 8 represents the ideal number, that is, it symbolizes the completion of the number of re-starting, which is why October 24 became a national UN Day. 

In that sense, you must think about how significant our historical posture and realistic position are, centered around our era. Since we have been planted in this main hall, even if it is difficult, we must be Unification Church members who can bloom our own flowers while proudly saying, "I am growing while humming a tune." Only then will the autumn harvest in the Unification Garden appear as a global harvest. In this sense, you must realize that blooming your own flowers is a serious issue. 

Therefore, for us, even a difficult path is not a difficult path. It is a path that must exist. 

The teacher has also thought this way, which is why he has overcome such crises every time. 

Then, what kind of person is the founder of the Unification Church? Is he a man disappearing under the persecution of the Republic of Korea through the three powers? Is he a man disappearing under the trials of three countries? Is he a man disappearing under the opposition of three denominations? He does not disappear. It is because he has remained through such trials that the Unification Church is in a position to see a new day of light in the world. In that sense, I hope that this morning will be a time for you to have new awareness and new determination. 

<Prayer> Please affirm our path, where we cannot confidently determine tomorrow's contract, with Your infinite patience and overcoming. If the loneliness of a day can guarantee eternity, then those who avoid that loneliness are extremely foolish. When we think that a moment of suffering can lay the foundation for eternity, it is only natural that those who dislike this cannot look at high-rise buildings. 

Even if we have loneliness and environments to overcome, if they become the foundation of hope where the country and the world can live, we must become Your beloved sons and daughters who strive infinitely to leave the conditions for tomorrow with a strong heart, firmly defending that position amidst hope and aspiration. 

Since we have already taken the step, when we think that one of two paths will be determined as either becoming left behind or becoming successful, we know that the fearful and astonishing path is connected from this very place where we stand today. We must not receive anyone's advice; rather, we must stand in a self-determined and self-reliant position, discovering ourselves who can encourage ourselves and commit ourselves. 

When we think about the spring, summer, autumn, and winter seasons in the era of the Unification Church, we anticipate the spring garden of a new nation and a new heaven and earth that is approaching, the new historical spring season, and the new bonds of life that can harmonize heaven and earth. I am certain that God has promised this in front of the path the Unification Church is taking today. 

If we are to go straight down that path, we must pave the expressway. There is a road that requires immense sacrifice and immense tears. When this road is paved, even if many people tell us to take another path, they will not be able to help but invest their own compassion and walk this road. When we realize that the glorious days promised to us will remain even after all the resources we have invested are taken away, we will know that we must shed all the sweat we have and put in all the sincerity we have. 

As people come and go, they must bow their heads in gratitude before our solemn and sacrificial spirit, saying that they too will inherit such a tradition and that they must walk such a path in thought. We must be a group that resolves to do so, even while running in a car. Therefore, until now, God has been sacrificing the church to pave the way for the nation, and sacrificing the nation to pave the way for the world, centered around the Republic of Korea, and we are at a point where we can see this with our living eyes. 

Today, we are at a solemn point where we can influence global issues centered around the situation of the Republic of Korea, and at the same time, we are at a solemn point where we can influence the world centered around the religion of the Republic of Korea. When we think about how the time has come to make decisions not from a discerning position but from a place where we are united in one focus, we must realize that it is indeed time to make the final resolution and the final commitment, the final oath and the final awareness, and the final determination. 

To become a group that does not perish in our inadequate form, we must become the Unification warriors who emerge with a self-reliant appearance that is not ashamed of the historical path through the inner and outer resolutions and oaths that no ancestors of any historical era had. We must not become a group that ignores this undeniable fact and deserves punishment. We must not do so even if we die. 

When I leave behind a grave after I die, I must be prepared to collapse in that place where the land of my desired homeland embraces me, and I earnestly ask and wish that we become heavenly warriors who will not hesitate to break through the path of suffering and adversity. 

Please remember Your children scattered across the nation today, and may You personally embrace and bless the countless children who call Your name in the embrace of unification and long for this place. 

May this day become a glorious day. I earnestly ask that Korea becomes a remembered country that can be admired by all nations of the world. 

When we think about what our position in this era is, we must run with joy, joy, and joy. Until the time our lives end, may we be Your sons and daughters who leave behind the path of destiny that we must cross with joy. I ask this once again, and I offer all these words in the name of the True Parents. Amen. *
